***нырнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нырнуть.html>нырну́ть</a> (5093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nьrǫ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁én</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">нирıати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nirıati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be"><a href = vnd.unilang:нырок.html>ны́рка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nýrka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">ни́рна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nírna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нырнуть.html>нырну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nyrnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нырять.html>ныря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dive</li></ol>

***ныть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ныть.html>ныть</a> (5216)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nyti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to yearn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ныть.html>ныть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to whimper, to whine, to yammer, to snivel, to bellyache, to cry <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to complain peevishly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to ache</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нюхать.html>ню́хать</a> (8470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нюхать.html>ню́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">njúxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понюхать.html>поню́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smell, to sniff</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнюхивать.html>обню́хивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">obnjúxivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нюха́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">njuxátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***нянька.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нька</a> (10539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нька</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">njánʹka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́ньки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́ньки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́ня</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njánja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семи́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нек</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дитя.html>дитя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>гла́за</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U semí <b>njánek</b> ditjá bez gláza.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Too many cooks spoil the broth. / Everybody's business is nobody's business. (Russian proverb)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нька</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заботиться.html>забо́тится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>двух</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:младенец.html>младе́нцах</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Njánʹka</b> zabótitsja o dvux mladéncax.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A (young) <b>nanny</b> looks after two infants.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***няня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́ня</a> (6583)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Since ancient times, from reduplication in children’s speech. The related form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нянька.html>ня́нька</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">njánʹka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was first attested in the 12th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">njánja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:няня.html>ня́нь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nurse</li>
<li>nanny</li>
<li>babysitter</li></ol>

***о.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> (33)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Letter_4">Letter</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">o</span>) (<i>lower case</i>, <i>upper case</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The sixteenth letter of the Russian Cyrillic alphabet.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">o</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The Cyrillic letter <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">O</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The Roman letter O, o.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_3">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">o</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>oh
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>О</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́же</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>O</b> bóže!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Oh God!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_2">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*o(b)</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃ebʰi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">o</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(+ prepositional case) about, of, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja čitál <b>o</b> njóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’ve read about him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (+ accusative case) against, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">opirátʹsja <b>o</b> sténu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lean against the wall</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> form is unstressed except in the idiom <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a> о́‎ <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bok ó‎ bok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>When governing the prepositional case, the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used before consonants, except before a few clusters where the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обо.html>обо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used.</li>
<li>When governing the accusative, the form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used before most consonants in the written language: the usage is variable before liquids. In the spoken language, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used in all cases.</li></ul>

***об.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> (127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*o(b)</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃ebʰi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ob</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ prepositional case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> about, of, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:узнать.html>узна́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:икра.html>икре́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja uznál mnógo <b>ob</b> ikré</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I found out a lot <b>about</b> caviar.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> against, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опираться.html>опира́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">opirátʹsja <b>ob</b> oknó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lean <b>against</b> the window</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> form is usually unstressed. It is stressed in the idioms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>рука́</a> о́‎б <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ruká ó‎b rúku</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> о́‎б <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горох.html>горо́х</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kak ó‎b stenu goróx</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. It can be stressed or unstressed in the word combination <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о́‎б <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>пол</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ó‎b pol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> по́‎л</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob pó‎l</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).</li>
<li>When governing the prepositional case, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> is used before vowels. However, both <i><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a></i> can occur before the <i>possessive</i> pronoun <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>When governing the accusative case, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> is used before vowels and variably before liquids in the written language. In the colloquial language, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a></i> is used before all words.</li></ul>
<hr />
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>Испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гласный.html>гла́сными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>зву́ками</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>



</ol>
</body>

***оба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a> (344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oba</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂e(m)bʰoh₁</i>, whence also Lithuanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">abu</i>, Latvian abi, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ambo</i> and Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄμφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ámphō</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">óbe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>both</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The usage pattern is the same as that found with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>:
<ul><li><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative or accusative case govern the genitive singular of the noun. While the noun in a nominative construction is in the genitive singular following <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an intervening adjective will be in the genitive plural (if masculine or neuter) or nominative plural (if feminine):
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стол.html>стола́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>óba</b> bélyx stolá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">both white tables</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>óba</b> nóvyx okná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">both new windows</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́шие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>óbe</b> xoróšije knígi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">both good books</span></div></li></ul></li>
<li>In the other cases, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óba</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́бе</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and any intervening adjective must all agree with the case of the noun:
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>обо́ими</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сскими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́тами</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>obóimi</b> rússkimi soldátami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with both Russian soldiers</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>обе́их</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́гах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ob <b>obéix</b> anglíjskix knígax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">about both English books</span></div></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li>The masculine genitive singular form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>обо́его</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obójevo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is an anomaly that sees only limited use:
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>обо́его</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пол.html>по́ла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obójevo</b> póla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">of both sexes</span></div></li></ul></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***обалдеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обалдеть.html>обалде́ть</a> (9567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>балда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">baldá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обалдеть.html>обалде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obaldétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обалдева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stop thinking clearly, to take leave of one's senses</li>
<li>to grow dumb with astonishment, to be dumb-founded, to drop one's jaw
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обалдеть.html>обалде́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:можно.html>мо́жно</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obaldétʹ</b> móžno!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it's enough to drive one crazy!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ние</a> (11834)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obajánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обаяние.html>обая́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>attraction, charm, fascination, spell (quality of inspiring delight or admiration)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обвали́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obvalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обвалиться.html>обвали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obvalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обва́ливаться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall, to collapse, to cave in, to crumble</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обвести.html>обвести́</a> (5327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">об-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ob-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обвести.html>обвести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обводить.html>обводи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">someone around</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to encircle, to surround</li>
<li>to outline, to contour
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:обвести.html>обвести́</a></b> чертёж <a href = vnd.unilang:тушь.html>ту́шью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obvestí</b> čertjóž túšʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ink in a drawing; outline a sketch in ink</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dodge, to outplay</li></ol>
